3 param area
M: f: 1 auto
2 dir
3 trig
4 sub
Met 1/2 n/p: Method: Using trigonometric identities
1. Use power-reduction identities: sin^m(x)cos^n(x) = sum of cos(kx).
2. So I = Int[-1/2*cos(4*x) + 1/4*cos(8*x) + 1/4] dx
3. Integrate each term separately.
4. Int[-1/2*cos(4*x)] dx = -1/8*sin(4*x)
5. Int[1/4*cos(8*x)] dx = 1/32*sin(8*x)
6. Int[1/4] dx = 1/4*x
7. = -1/8*sin(4*x) + 1/32*sin(8*x) + 1/4*x + C

4. Int[-1/2*cos(2*(5*x - 5))] dx = -1/20*sin(2*(5*x - 5))
5. Int[1/4*cos(4*(5*x - 5))] dx = 1/80*sin(4*(5*x - 5))
6. Int[1/4] dx = 1/4*x

10. Simplify.
